EFTA00006398

This document page is a detailed itemized billing statement for telecommunications charges. It appears to be a printout from a phone service provider's customer account. The page is structured as a table with the following columns: Date, Call Destination, Time, Number Called, Call Type, Minutes, Airtimes Charges, Toll Charges, and Total. The data is primarily for calls made on June 20, 2006, most of which are local calls to White Plains, NY, and a few to New York, NY. ## Analysis

## Key Features

1. **Header Information**
   - The top of the page includes:
     - "Itemized Details For:" followed by redacted account information.
     - "Customer Service Number" with the number `1-800-937-8997` clearly visible.
     - Date: `Jul 21, 2006`
     - Page indicator: `Page 71 of 97`

2. **Main Table**
   - Title: `LOCAL AIRTIME, LONG DISTANCE and INTERNATIONAL CHARGES - (Continued)`
   - This indicates the page is a continuation of a larger list of charges.
   - Columns:
     - Date
     - Call Destination
     - Time
     - Number Called (redacted with black bars)
     - Call Type (all entries marked as `(F)` — Mobile2Mobile)
     - Minutes
     - Airtime Charges (all `$ -`)
     - Toll Charges (all `$ -`)
     - Total (all `$ -`)

   - The table lists numerous calls made on July 9th and 10th, 2006, mostly to White Plains, New York, and New York, NY. The calls are very short (mostly 1 minute) and are marked as “Mobile2Mobile”, suggesting they were made between phones on the same carrier. Airtime and toll charges are shown as zero.

3. **Call Type Legend**
   - Located at the bottom of the table, providing definitions for the call type codes (A through V).

4. **Footer/Document ID**
   - The bottom right corner shows the identifier: `EFTA00006449`

This page is a standard, structured document — an itemized phone bill detail — not a photograph or diagram. The content is clearly intended to be read as a structured list of billing information, making it a functional document for tracking usage and charges.
